 Testosterone hormone: If the balance of this hormone present in the body is disturbed, it can lead to many diseases
 is hormone kaa badhanaa or ghatana donon hi sharir ke liye nuksaandaayak hota he
 If the level of this hormone is high, you may have many problems
 jaise vajan badhanaa, sar ke bal jhadanaa, keel munhaase aadi
 Whereas the decrease of this hormone causes breast cancer and heart related diseases
 thyroid hormone:yah hormone hamaare sharir main ek granthi ke saamaan hota he, is granthi se paidaa hone vaale hormone insaan kii kaary karne kii kshamta par asar daalate hai
